<Rating>4< /Rating><review>This Banquet Hall is nice and fresh inside. The bathrooms are clean and well maintained. Food was good and the waiter service was great! They were friendly, generous, and have alot to offer. I am amazed how much food and drinks they had throughout the entire night. I also enjoyed the LED dancefloor and the lighting, it really brings that club vibe in. However, the sound system and DJ was THE WORST I'VE EVER HEARD. The speakers sounded terrible with excessive highs. The DJ had a cheap 90 dollar console with him and barely knew how to mix the songs together. Then, repeated the same words over and over again when talking on the mic. Overall, very unprofessional. Now the parking was not convenient but I don't blame the venue. Overall, great Banquet Hall. If it wasn't for the sound system and DJ, I would of given this place 5 Stars. For anyone booking this banquet hall, I highly suggest bringing in a different DJ. Two big comments for those looking at coming here: if you have renters insurance already, check to see if it covers storage units and bring those details or you will have to get a policy there.  And second: the little units sit above bigger units, so if you plan on putting heavy objects in there, ensure you can comfortably carry it up a flight of stairs and lift it into a space on your own< /text>

<Review>If you think storage should be convenient, or you want to get access to your stuff *Don't rent here*.
The staff are very polite (but *not* helpful), the facility is clean, and fairly secure.  But they are VERY, VERY, serious about their rules (Think; stalinist communism, or the DMV).

They will *not*  give any warning ,  and they will *not* discuss the matter with you, They will kick you out at the, first discovered event  (I say discovered because people break the rules all the time they just don't notice )

You will be given *2 DAYS* to find a new storage, rent a truck, and move (I had to move three truck loads), or they will repossess or trash can your stuff.

Do not stay late !!!!!!!!!
Do not smoke on permis (even in the parking lot , you have to go to the sidewalk)
Do not leave trash ( and I mean any trash !)
Do not  use the facility trash bin ( you have to pack it out in your car)
Do not store any unacceptable items (I.E. furniture ONLY! )
Do not park overnight ( They will absolutely tow you )

Do not get LOCKED OUT ( if you do you have both stayed late, and parked over night a double whammy, and even though there is an on site manager, there is no way to reach her, you have to call corporate office.)

Any of these, will get you booted

I got busted for staying late, which I was told was " trespassing" and "endangering the life of the of [public storage] employes ".  and she was VERY much serious.

Now if you mind you manners , and watch you P's and Q's, you can store your stuff there ( I was paying 213.00 a month), but if you don't :(  It's there way -or- the highway.

So in my opinion it's better just to go down the street, there are plenty of places to store. (I liked Stor-All I had a pretty good experience with them.)

Jeff Toll, MD is the general practitioner behind Same Day Testing. Please read the other 1-star review below, as I and multiple others I know have had the same experience. This is clearly insurance fraud.

I paid $50 upfront for a rapid test and added my insurance information.
Same Day Testing sent my insurance a $600 claim for the following additional services... "Addtl supplies materials & clinical staff time". This is clearly fraud- I only went for a nasal swab covid test and left.

Under the terms of my policy, my insurance only covered $88 of the bill, and requested that I paid the remaining $512... I called my insurance and disputed the amount, and I had my insurance rep speak with Same Day Testing. Same Day Testing told my insurance that they would drop the $512 so long as the additional $88 was paid.

My issue with all of this is that the cost of the rapid test WITHOUT insurance is $125. Why is the cost of the test HIGHER WITH insurance, $133 ($50+$88)?? This doctor and same day testing are deliberately ripping people and insurance companies off, trying to take advantage of the people who don't take the time to dispute the charge.</review>

< Text>
my wife got a Covid test covered by our insurance.  They required a physician, assigned to us. The problem here is an egregious billing by Dr. Toll.  $600 for essentially doing nothing.  the insurance company absorbs this cost and this is why the cost of health care in this country is out of control. Why?

Like many, I went into my first appointment with skepticism because of terrible experiences at other dental offices. < Review>
Look no further for a friendly and thorough dentist office. This was my first visit to this office and I absolutely loved it! I really like the location, it's on 1st floor of a nice, clean office building. Parking was very easy and the office was not hard to find at all. As soon as I walked into the office I would immediately greeted by a group of friendly front desk receptionists. I was asked to sign in and I provided them with copies of my paperwork that was emailed to me for completion ahead of time.

I waited approximately five minutes before the dental assistant greeted me and gave me a tour of their office facilities and introduced me to some of their staff. All X-rays are completed using digital technologies (no film required). I was seated in the dental chair about 10 mins before Dr. Joyce Tse arrived to examine my X-rays. She thoroughly explained what she was looking at, her concerns, and proper maintenance of my teeth. Prior to my teeth cleaning, she gave me a pair of cool goggles to put on, to prevent water from splashing onto my eyes during the procedure. She was gentle and thorough, checking on me every quad to make sure I was still good and alive. No pain whatsoever.

I left their office with a cool goody bag. They have lip balms at the front for patients to take-smells good and it works! I left their office pretty happy with a plan on my next set of treatments.< /Review>

<Review>I was very skeptical about using this flower shop, just because I have called and placed orders at about 4 different flowers shops this year and have not been one bit happy with any of the floral arrangements that were delivered. All I can say is that my search for a flower shop is finally over!! I had flowers delivered to my mother today and she called me as soon as she received them and told me that, from all of the flowers that I have ever sent her, these were the most beautiful ones she has ever received!! She said that all of the flowers were beautiful, colorful, fresh looking and smelt incredible, unlike the other flowers that she has received in the past from other flower shops where they had brown edges or missing petals. She also loved the purple vase the flowers came in, said it was a different touch/look from the regular clear ginger vase that flowers usually come in. I asked my mom to send me a picture of the arrangement and I was wowed when I received the picture. I literally went back into Edelweiss' website to pull up the picture of the arrangement that I had ordered (Teleflora's Fresh Flourish Bouquet) and pulled up my mom's picture of the flowers that she received today and put both pictures side by side. All I can say is that my mom received exactly what I payed and hoped for!! Every single flower was arranged EXACTLY as it did on the picture of their website. It was an exact replica!! All the other flower shops that I used in the past never sent me the exact arrangement as what was shown on their website. Edelweiss' website has the actual measurements of each arrangement and my moms' flowers were the exact size as what was mentioned on their website!! <text>*UPDATE TO FIRST REVIEW*

My family and I decided to try to give this place another shot because truth be told the food and drinks are pretty great. We went on a Tuesday night and the parking lot was pretty full but it looked like there was a table or two that was empty. I got up to the hostess stand and asked how long the wait would be for a party of four plus a high chair and was told 20 to 25 minutes. This was at 7:47 p.m. They close at 9:00 p.m. So I decided to give her my name and number just in case a table opens sooner . We decided to go to Dollar Tree in the same parking lot and look around. We literally pulled up to the Dollar Tree and were about to get out of the car when I received a text (7:48) stating that the table was ready. So the hostess intentionally tried to get me to leave by giving me a time frame that was nowhere near correct when in fact there was as I believed a table available for my family.

My husband hadn't been here before and was so turned off at the fact that the employee intentionally lied so that we wouldn't wait for a table that we ended up just leaving. We like to enjoy dinner out with our family but this establishment does not deserve any of our hard-earned money. They need to train their employees to treat guests better. The fact that there was a table available for us and the hostess completely and blatantly lied shows what kind of establishment that this. As I've said before the food and drinks are good but we will not be visiting here ever again and would not recommend to anyone that I know.

1st Review..

Food and drinks were amazing! They would have been given 5 stars if their service wasn't absolutely horrible. However, because the food and drinks were so good..I MAY consider paying another visit.

We had a group of 6 + a baby. On a very busy Saturday night. With Covid-19, outdoor seating only. We had one person in the group order a soda and everyone received their alcoholic beverages before the soda. I ordered a bean dip as an appetizer and we only had a few chips left so you would think that they would bring out a fresh basket of chips with the bean dip. NOPE, after repeated requests for chips, they never came! I finally just asked them to remove the bean dip off of my ticket because we didn't get a chance to enjoy it because we never received the chips. Out of the six of us that ordered one person did not receive their meal at all. It seems as if they forgot to put it on the ticket or didn't add it to the ticket and by the time she received her food although it was delicious everyone was pretty much done with their plate.

I also had a 10 month old baby in a high chair. Even though the table was pretty full. The waitress still chose to put HOT plates of food in front of the baby when I asked her to hand them to me so I can put them on the side. When it came time to pay, they put everything on one check. You could clearly see that the table was full of six adults that were not together. When we sat down we told them it was individual checks. The waitress that was helping us was so rude that she didn't even come to collect the checks or to thank us. We did have a helpful server by the name of Jessie who took our checks and payments and received an additional tip just because of his politeness.

Overall if you're looking for good food and good drinks then you're at the right place. If you go out to receive a good dining experience with a great wait staff then this may not be the place for you. If you can overlook the atrociousness and rudeness of the waitresses who leave in the middle of taking a drink order then you're good. The female manager was pretty rude too.

For the record, I ordered a Mocajete (came out sizzling hot and fresh), their tortillas are delicious, a few other people had a 2 item combo. Their only complaint was dryness and the staff ignoring the sauce and water request. To sum it up, go at your own risk.<//text></record>

< Text>
I've been going to Agave Azul for a couple of years (mostly takeout because it's on the way home from work) and every meal has been fantastic.  The Burrito Supreme and California Burrito are awesome and huge! They've redecorated the main dining area and completely updated and improved the bar. <UserId.>118292809227997360016< /UserId.><user_name>Scott Peterson< /user_name>< time>
1484773532329<//time>
< rating>
5<//rating>
< text>
Traveling for business and stumbled into this place randomly.  I don't pull out 5 stars very often, but I just ate the best burrito that I've ever had.  I don't say that lightly, as I've lived all over California and experienced some pretty incredible Mexican food.
The "healthy" burrito here was mouth watering.  Every aspect of it from the green sauce to each veggie in it, to the choice of cheese was well thought out and equally well prepared.
I can only hope the rest of the menu is as good.  The cooks here know what they are doing.
I sat in the very attractive bar and was well tended to.  Not sure if the experience would be different in the main seating area.
Overall, super surprised and very pleased.  I will go out of my way to come back.</text>

< Review>
Service is usually not that good, last time I was there it was probably the worst service I've ever had anywhere.

Agave Azul is the closest restaurant to my house, but I don't know if I'll ever go back. My pal and I showed up at about 8pm and the bar was pretty full, so we asked the bartender if we could sit out on the patio, doing so mostly to ensure he knew we would be out there. After sitting out there for 15 minutes and no sign of anyone coming out to take our drink order I went in to order drinks at the bar. I thought that might be easier for them since they were busy. After about 10 minutes of trying to get the same bartender to acknowledge me, he asks if I'm the group on the patio and says that they just sent a server from the restaurant out to take our order. He then left the bar area and did not care at all to take my drink order.

At that time I am pretty irritated, but whatever. I go back outside and my buddy says she brought chips/salsa and said she would be right back to take our order. It took another 15 minutes until we saw her again. So 40 minutes in to our visit and we are just now putting in an order for drinks, and we order food at the same time because we can't risk letting her go back in. Sometime during this whole event a pair of ladies had sat down at the next table over. Well I am telling my first time visiting friend that although the service is never great it is not usually this terrible. I probably used some semi-colorful language, but in a private conversation.  So fast forward another 15 or 20 minutes and our food comes out to our table. A few minutes later, finally, our drinks come out. So an hour or so in to our visit and we finally have a Cadillac margarita and a tall Pacifico. Nothing extravagant. But it somehow took 20 minutes after we ordered them, 40 minutes after we sat down. So we eat, we hang out for a bit, I use the bathroom while we are waiting for the check. As I walk back through the bar I ask about our check and our waitress comes around and say that the owner heard there were some complaints and that they have covered our visit. I asked several times if I can still pay the tab as I don't have cash on me and would like to still tip the server. She was fine and did her job. She then tells us that the owner was seated a table over and heard everything we said.

I wasn't really that upset about our visit even though the service was super slow. But at that time my pal requested to speak to the owner, he was half wanting to thank her and half wanting to apologize for complaining too loud in our conversation. Well.... She came out with her arms folded and mad at us like we were out of line to complain amongst ourselves. We never once complained to an employee or anyone at the restaurant.  It was a completely worthless conversation trying to express our regret that she heard our complaints, I am not the type of person that will complain to an establishment, and I do not want to receive free stuff. She told us that it was busy and they did the best they could by sending a server out to our table and that she handled the bill for us, rudely. I seriously went in to the bar to save them the trip outside only to get blown off and have to wait even longer. After all that I was more irritated by her conversation and tone than by the service.

I don't normally write such poor reviews on local businesses. I'm well aware of how hard it can be to be a small business owner. In this instance, though, I don't think I will be going back there and everyone who I have told my experience to has had the same sort of response. "The service is not great but we like to food". That is pretty much how my wife and I have always felt. And I can deal with that.

I won't deal with being rude and pushing it back on me as a customer when your service is beyond slow and I have an issue with it.<//Review>

Found this place driving to Oakdale. Homemade tortillas, good portions and pretty quick service. We've been there for lunch and dinner and left full and happy each time.
I just had the chorizo and eggs breakfast special and it was fantastic. The side of fruit was strawberries, big raspberries and blood oranges. Colorful and tasty.
This has become our favorite Mexican food in the area, and we have tried them all.< /review>
